# WOOperationsPVO

## 📌 Visão Geral

View Object para extração BICC de dados de WOOperations. Acessa as tabelas: CSE_CONDITION_EVENT_CODES_B, EGP_SYSTEM_ITEMS_B_V, POR_REQUISITION_HEADERS_ALL (+21).

**Caminho:** `FscmTopModelAM.WorkOrderAM.WOOperationsPVO`

| Atributos | Tabelas | PKs | BICC | BICC % |
|-----------|---------|-----|------|--------|
| 3170 | 24 | 1 | 624 | 20% |
